##############################################################Changing resources into icons and sorting

	Resources := sort_text@(order: "67891234") +
		# step 1 : remove all automatic tags
		tag_remove_rule(tag: "<sym-auto>") +
		# step 2 : symbols
		replace_rule(
			match: "[|1|2|3|4|6|7|8|9|]",
			replace: "<sym-auto>&</sym-auto>" )
				
##############################################################Calculating base CV

	cv_to_num := {
		if input == "1" then 1
		else if input == "2" then 2
		else if input == "3" then 3
		else if input == "4" then 4
		else if input == "5" then 5
		else if input == "6" then 6
		else if input == "7" then 7
		else if input == "8" then 8
		else if input == "9" then 9
		else 0
		}
	cv1and2 := { cv_to_num(card.CV) * 10 + cv_to_num(card.CV1) }

##############################################################Special word are written from big letters

	upperwords := { check(card.Action) }
